This not only reduces the possibility of card fraud, but also makes capturing and storing smartcard details much quicker and more efficient. \r\n\r\nThis app works online, accessing the most up-to-date information, as well as offline. (If the photo shown does not match the one shown on the front of the actual card, it has probably been tampered with and may be a fake card.);\r\n5.\tTouch the Card Details tab to view the list of current qualifications.\r\n6.\tDo the same with more smartcards if you need to.\r\n\r\n\r\nTo read a virtual smartcard:\r\n\r\n1.\tOpen the app;\r\n2.\tTouch the 'SCAN A QR CODE' button;\r\n3.\tRead the QR code (from approx. 10cm away);\r\n4.\tAn image of the card appears.
